When the car reached the halfway point, one of the customers instructed the driver to first drive the car to Nanyang Bridge to pick up a guest. When they arrived there, three more male guests got into the car. At this time, there were six people in the car, including the driver. Yin accelerated and headed towards Longhua. When they reached Xielu on Zhongshan Road, one of them suddenly ordered the car to stop. The one dressed as a mechanic and two others jumped out of the car, took out box cannons, and forced the driver out of the car. Two of them grabbed Yin's arms and moved him forward into the field. The one with the gun followed closely to monitor and prevent him from looking back. At the time, Yin had no choice but to obey. He heard the engine start and expected the car to be driven away. After walking about half a li, the two who were holding Yin released him and retreated, telling him not to look back. After another quarter of an hour, Yin looked back and all three of them were gone. Yin was slightly calmer at this time and rushed to the nearby Xujiahui Public Security Bureau to report the incident. Soon after, all the police stations in the Public Concession and the French Concession received the report. It was not until around noon that the car was found south of the Cade Theatre on Cade Road. As for the purpose of robbing the car, it is currently under investigation.

At this moment, all the detectives rushed forward, subdued him, and seized the iron awl. The final search resulted in the arrest of six individuals. The first, who wielded the awl, was named Lin Zhao (25 years old, from Fujian). The others were Chen Chuncheng (25 years old, from Wenzhou), Huang Puwen (58 years old, from Wenzhou), Lin Jian'an (37 years old, from Wenzhou), Mei Yunguang (38 years old, from Pingyang), and Wei Shun (26 years old, from Fujian). Using Hand Grenades as Weapons to Intimidate and Seize Goods 135

Perpetrated at Least Six Cases - Zhou Taibing is a True Scourge of Society

Zhou Taibing, from Zhenjiang, is twenty-two years old this year and resides at No. 19 Yangzhou Road in the Public Concession. On the afternoon of July 13th of last year at 3:00 PM, he went to Quan Tai, a wool, flannel, silk, and foreign goods store at No. 362 Avenue Edward VII, to purchase goods. The shop assistant, Shen Jisheng, attended to the transaction. Zhou immediately selected various clothing materials, totaling seventy-nine yuan and fifty cents. After cutting and wrapping them, he instructed Shen to issue an invoice for payment. As Shen turned to prepare the invoice at the accounts desk, Zhou seized the opportunity to take out a hand grenade from his pocket and hold it in his hand. He also produced a letter signed "Iron-Blooded Assassination Corps" and placed it on the counter, loudly declaring to the shop assistants, "I'm going to throw a grenade, quickly get away!" Upon seeing Zhou produce the grenade and witnessing his intention to throw it, the shop assistants naturally fled in panic. Zhou then grabbed the package of purchased clothing materials and fled. Later, Yu Ruilin, the manager of the store, filed a report with the French Concession Police, requesting an investigation, but without success. It is understood that Zhou subsequently habitually impersonated the "Iron-Blooded Assassination Corps," writing threatening letters and, in the same manner, defrauding clothing materials and goods from various foreign goods stores in the Public Concession. He would first trick them into cutting materials and goods, then produce a grenade and threatening letter, grabbing the goods and fleeing. He committed the same crime in at least six cases. After the stores reported to the police, requesting an investigation, Zhou was finally apprehended by the Public Concession Police. A hand grenade was confiscated and he was sent to the First Special Court for prosecution and trial. He was sentenced to seven years in prison. After investigation by the French Concession Police, a request was submitted to the Second Special Court to dispatch detectives Li Jinzhang and Xu Songlin to transfer Zhou, along with the hand grenade, from the First Special Court to the Second Special Court, Criminal Division One. Presiding Judge Xiong Huitui conducted the hearing. Police lawyer Fei Xizhen presented the case, requesting a postponement to allow for a detailed investigation into whether the defendant had committed other crimes, and then proceed with the trial. Yu Ruilin, the manager of the plaintiff, Quan Tai, testified about the defendant's fraudulent acquisition of goods, intimidation, and fleeing with the goods. Zhou Taibing confessed that he had served as a volunteer soldier during the January 28th Incident and that he had brought back the hand grenade upon discharge. He claimed that it had been submerged in water and was not explosive. He also admitted to falsely claiming to be the "Iron-Blooded Assassination Corps" to intimidate and defraud goods without denial. The court verified the confession and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody for another hearing on the 22nd.

Xu Hongsheng, a native of Nantong, aged fifty-four, residing in a flat at No. 10 Zhangjiazhai, located between Edinburgh Road and Carter Road in the Public Concession, currently works as a waiter at a Western restaurant at No. 1958 Avenue Joffre and Route Ferguson in the French Concession. It was confirmed that the deceased had died from heart disease. The judge ordered the family to sign a guarantee before claiming the body for burial.

Additionally, 3,800 yuan is needed for the daughter Rongfang's education in middle school and university, totaling 44,100 yuan. Due to the current financial difficulties and accumulating debts, he requested that the court first order the payment of 800 yuan and declare provisional execution. Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau Prohibits Export of Tea Leaves Dyed with Toxic Colors 143

Implementation to Begin This Year

The coloring of tea leaves should be prohibited. However, due to continued demand in foreign markets, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, after considering the situation, approved temporary exports. While colored tea had not yet been completely banned, efforts were made to ensure that the colorants were pure and non-toxic, so as not to affect hygiene. Experts also researched various yellow colorants for manufacturing and sale, which were widely used. The bureau recently discovered that some colored tea leaves for export were still dyed with lead-based chrome and other yellow powders, which not only harmed human health but also potentially affected international trade and hindered sales. A notice was issued to tea merchants stating that from this year onwards, all new tea for export that required coloring should use non-toxic alternatives. The use of copper-based chrome and other toxic colorants will be strictly prohibited. Tea merchants are cautioned not to attempt to use them.

Corpse Dismemberment and Destruction Case - Court Exhumes Body 145

Flesh and Bones Rotting, Horrific to Behold - Head Not Yet Found, Still Awaiting Excavation

Gong Shaoting, the owner of the Gong Hongtai Construction Factory at the Gongxing Road Bridge Pier on Baoxing Road in Zhabei, colluded with his mistress, a local woman named Hou, on the evening of March 12th of last year to lure his former mistress, Gu Aqiao, to Hou's residence on the upper floor of No. 37 Shun Da Lane, Keming Road. There, they strangled Gu Aqiao to death with a rope. Afterwards, they buried Aqiao's body in the third courtyard of the Gong Hongtai Construction Factory on Baoxing Road. Later, Gong Shaoting, Hou, and Gong's son-in-law, Shen Fufu, felt that this was inappropriate. In early May of last year, they instructed a worker, Zhou Baoquan, to enlist the help of Li Baosheng and Gui Sheng. At night, they dug up Aqiao's body, chopped it into three pieces with an axe - the head, torso, and waist. They packed the pieces into sacks, sealed them tightly with lime, and placed them in baskets. They moved the head and buried it in an open space in front of the Zhu Jiazhai residence. The torso and waist were buried under the back door of the third room of the newly built flat, intending to make everything foolproof and carefree. However, the net of heaven is vast, with meshes large but letting nothing through. Xie Baolin, the nephew of the deceased, who lived at No. 5 Dingfeng Lane, Ba Xianqiao in the French Concession, noticed something amiss. He reported the matter to Lu Ying, the captain of the Investigation Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting him to send officers to investigate thoroughly. Upon receiving the report, Captain Lu instructed squad leaders Zhou Peichuan and Chen Guangyan to lead detectives to search in different directions. The truth was revealed, and the masterminds Gong Shaoting, Hou, and the murderers Zhou Baoquan and Li Baosheng were arrested one after another. After separate rigorous interrogations, each confessed without hesitation. They were sent to the Third Section for transfer to the local court for handling. It was reported previously. It is now learned that after the case was transferred to the local court, the court dispatched prosecutor Lei and forensic doctor Zhao Huachu, along with court police Xu Guoguang and Shen Tingfang, and Investigation Team squad leaders Zhou and Chen from the Public Security Bureau, accompanied by detectives Lu Zhenyuan and others, and the local headman Yan Liugen. They brought the accomplice Zhou Baoquan to the Gong Hongtai Construction Factory at No. 933 West Baoxing Road in Zhabei at approximately 11:00 AM yesterday, traveling by car. At 12:30 PM, the police officers, along with the police chief of the Bazihqiao Police Station of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, supervised the excavation of the earth at the back door of the third courtyard. At approximately 2:00 PM, after digging to a depth of five to six feet, the deceased's blue leather jacket and linen bag with arms were discovered. By 4:30 PM, the body had been completely exhumed. The flesh and bones were already rotting, making it horrific to behold. A telephone call was made to prosecutor Lei, who arrived at the scene to inspect. However, the head had been abandoned elsewhere in a public cemetery and its whereabouts were unknown. Therefore, prosecutor Lei sealed the body and ordered the headman to guard it. He also ordered squad leaders Zhou Peishan and Yang Guangyan to continue investigating the whereabouts of the head. It is heard that Gong Shaoting, Hou, Zhou Baoquan, and others, who are in custody at the court, will be temporarily returned to the Public Security Bureau for detention in order to facilitate the search for the head.

Zheng Jianbo and Others Organize the Citizens' National Goods Consumption Association 146

Yesterday, a request was submitted to the City Party Headquarters for filing.

Shiye She reports: Zheng Jianbo, former Commander-in-Chief of the Volunteer Army Transportation Corps of the four northeastern provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe, recently gathered more than 30 patriotic comrades in Shanghai and organized the Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Consumption Association on the third floor of Taichangfangzi on Zhejiang Road. The aim is to set an example by using national goods, and to persuade all households, shops, schools, factories, etc., in the city to use national products as much as possible to recover rights and interests. No membership fees will be charged. The association yesterday submitted a request to the City Party Headquarters for filing. The original text states, "Regarding the organization of the Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Consumption Association, we earnestly request approval for filing. Jianbo and others, recognizing the decline of industry and the stagnation of national goods, believe that all of us citizens should shoulder the responsibility of actively promoting national goods. Since

Page 12

the opening of the five treaty ports, foreigners have been dumping foreign goods without end. The outflow of money is incalculable, leading to economic bankruptcy and the impoverishment of the people. The leak is not stopped, and recovery is impossible. Although there have been calls to promote national goods over the years, they have risen and fallen like the wind, but they are empty in name and lack practicality. Furthermore, there are still very few consumers, making it difficult to achieve results. Therefore, Jianbo and others gathered more than 30 comrades to initiate the organization of the Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Consumption Association, specifically to persuade all households, shops, schools, factories, etc., in the city to earnestly use national goods. The aim is to make all residents of the city realize that using national goods is an urgent and necessary measure, so that foreign goods will naturally be eliminated, the leak can be stopped, and the country can become rich and the people strong, all through this action. For this reason, we have prepared a document and attached a draft of the association's constitution and declaration on using national goods, and submit it to your department for review. We earnestly request approval for filing, as it is in the public interest."

International Journalists' Inspection Group Shanghai Members Went to Beijing Last Night 148

Returning to Shanghai at the end of this month.

Shenshi News Agency reports: The communist bandits in Jiangxi have recently been completely suppressed after being personally led by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who supervised the advance of a large army in multiple directions. Our military and diplomatic authorities, in order to make it clear to various countries the kind of destruction caused by the communist bandits and the reconstruction work after the recovery, specially initiated the organization of an international journalists' group to go to Jiangxi for inspection. There were a total of twenty participants, all of whom were reporters from various countries, including Britain, France, the United States, and Germany, stationed in China. According to inquiries from the Shenshi News Agency reporter, the reporters from various countries participating in Shanghai have already taken the train to Beijing at 11 o'clock last night. The Shenshi News Agency reporter has specially recorded the names of the members of the journalist group and the itinerary items as follows:

(Names of those traveling together) Participants from various countries in Shanghai include: Powell, editor of the Miller's Review; Gold, editor of the Greater Shanghai Evening Post; Victor Keeney, China correspondent for the New York Herald Tribune; Steele, reporter for the United Press; Smelts, Chicago correspondent in China; Halliwell, Heitong Telegraph Agency; Dr. Kepler, representative of the Berlin East Asia Forum; Captain Marx, representative of the Shanghai German Daily; Dr. Liberra, representative of the German Frankfurter Zeitung. (Proposed itinerary) The group is led by Wang Fudan of the National Society. After taking the train to Beijing, they will have breakfast at the International Friendship Society. At noon, they will be hosted by the Nanjing Daily Public Association. In the afternoon, they will visit various places. In the evening, they will be treated to dinner by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Tomorrow morning (the 16th), they will take the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Guangshun" to depart, and they will arrive in Jiujiang on the 17th. They will then go directly to Nanchang, and it is expected that they will arrive on the morning of the 18th. On the 20th, they will go to Linchuan, Nanfeng, Guangchang, Ningdu, and other places. On the 29th, they will take the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway back to Hangzhou, and return to Shanghai that night. The total itinerary is fifteen days.

The Municipal Government Rewards Citizens for Assisting in the Arrest of Robbers 149

According to a report from the Public Security Bureau to the Municipal Government, at 9:00 PM on November 10th, 23rd year of the Republic, police officer Zhang Zhongyuan of the Rihuqiao Police Station had his gun robbed. Ji Zitang pursued the crowd with few people and recovered the gun. This is deeply commendable. It is requested that a reward be given. After deliberation at the 275th Municipal Conference of the Municipal Government, it was determined that it was in accordance with the provisions of Article 3, Paragraph 1, Item 4, and Paragraph 2 of the Municipal Government's Medal Rules. Medals should be awarded separately to show encouragement. Reduce Camel Wool Intermodal Transport Price 150

A six-month trial period will be implemented from January 1st.

Camel wool transported from Baotou or Xi'an to Shanghai can be transported via Pinghan, Longhai, Beining, Jinpu, Jinghu, and Huhangyong railways, and the number of grades reduced by one grade according to the grade table is used as the direct freight rate. This case has been approved by the Ministry of Railways and will be implemented from January 1st of this year for a six-month trial period.

The Western Clothing Industry Guild Requests the Issuance of New Soft Rulers 151

Exemption from punishment if the new ruler is not issued.

The Western Clothing Industry Guild suggested to the authorities: "Regarding the request to consult the Bureau of Weights and Measures and expedite the issuance of new soft rulers for application and business purposes. It has been found that members of our guild use soft rulers to tailor Western clothing. Although the implementation of the new system of weights and measures has been in place for many years, soft rulers have not been sold on the market. Therefore, members of our guild have had no choice but to continue using the old soft rulers to conduct business. This is because our industry of tailoring Western clothing must measure the body size closely, and bamboo rulers are useless. Soft rulers are indispensable. Recently, we have received reports from fellow traders along Zhonghua Road in Nanshi, such as Fulou Company, Zhonghua, and Guohua, that they have been searched by your bureau in conjunction with the Public Security Bureau for using soft rulers, and have been notified by the local court for compulsory enforcement and punishment. Although members of our guild want to comply with the new system of measuring instruments, they cannot be purchased in reality. If we do not urgently seek remedies, then the old ones cannot be used and the new ones have not yet been issued. During this transition period, the business prospects of our industry will suffer great losses. Therefore, we have prepared this document and request that your bureau, considering the circumstances, expedite the consultation with the Bureau of Weights and Measures to issue new soft rulers for application. Before the issuance of the soft rulers, the old soft rulers will be temporarily allowed to be used to maintain business. We also request the local court to withdraw the order and exempt Fulou, Zhonghua, Guohua, and other companies from the punishment for using soft rulers to alleviate the merchants' difficulties, which would be a great kindness." Respectfully presented by Wu, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, and Wang Lianfang, Chairman of the Shanghai Western Clothing Industry Guild.

According to the Japanese Mainichi Shimbun, on the 12th of this month, when the Shanghai Maru entered Nagasaki, a Japanese merchant named Imabayashi, who runs a business on Peng Road in Shanghai, illegally transported a large number of precious stones to Japan. When the ship docked and was being quarantined, a third-class passenger, who looked dignified and like a gentleman, was seen by the customs officers disembarking for inspection, hastily trying to escape. He was seen by the dock manager, who suspected his behavior and ordered an inspection. A white gold-encrusted gem ring, two cat's eye rings, brooches, and other valuables worth several thousand yuan were found on him. He claimed, "I live at No. 160 Peng Road in Shanghai, named Imabayashi Matsutaro. These valuables were brought here at the request of others and are not my own. Therefore, I did not want to hide them in my shoes like others and secretly conceal them." After investigation by the authorities, it was determined that he was a habitual offender of smuggling and was taken into custody.

Chen Huazhang is Accused of Assaulting and Insulting Court Bailiffs 156

Chen Huazhang, a local resident living at No. 4 Raul East Road in the French Concession, is sixty years old and runs Shun Shengji Construction Factory. He has been dealing with the Shanghai Bank for loans. Because he owed more than 2,000 foreign dollars, he refused to pay. The Shanghai Bank filed a complaint with the Second Special Court for mediation, but it was unsuccessful. The bank then formally filed a lawsuit, requesting an investigation. The court issued a summons according to the complaint and sent bailiff Wang Zushao to Chen's residence on Raul East Road to deliver the summons. Unexpectedly, Chen replied that no one lived here. Wang, who did not know Chen, had no choice but to return to the court disappointed. He reported the information to the presiding judge Ma Yishu. By the time the court session began, only the plaintiff, Yang Jiemei, the agent of the Shanghai Bank, was present. The official ordered the plaintiff to designate the person to report to the court for another interrogation. Until the afternoon of December 28th of last year, at 3:00 PM, a Mr. Zou from the Shanghai Bank, accompanied by bailiff Wang, went to designate the person. Unexpectedly, Chen not only refused to accept the summons, but also assaulted and slapped bailiff Wang's face twice. Wang again reported the information to the court, and the court, because the defendant Chen Huazhang intentionally refused to appear in court, ruled in absentia. He still ordered bailiff Wang Shaozu to deliver the judgment. Wang was afraid of being insulted again, so he accompanied the bailiff to deliver it. When they arrived, Chen was lying across the bed in the room, inhaling opium. When Chen saw the bailiff and bailiff delivering the judgment, Chen threw the judgment on the ground and instigated the male and female guests in the room to besiege them. The bailiff and bailiff reported to the police station by Wang's phone and sent detectives to arrest them. Chen had already escaped in the meantime. Wang Shaozu, because Chen was so unreasonable and insulted public officials, which was related to the authority of the court, reported the information to the prosecutor's office and sent bailiffs to summon him to the address. However, Chen still refused to appear. Therefore, the chief prosecutor signed an arrest warrant and brought Chen to court. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Wang Ren and clerk Peng Yi specially opened the second court for interrogation. The defendant hired a lawyer to the court for discussion. First, the plaintiff Wang Shaozu said, "On the 28th of last month, I was ordered by Judge Ma to go to the defendant's home to deliver the summons. The defendant said that there was no Chen Huazhang and refused to accept the summons. The second time, the plaintiff sent someone to accompany me to designate the person. At that time, the defendant was lying on the bed and smoking opium, and spoke insults. The third time I went to deliver the summons, the defendant did not see me at first. When I walked out of the alley, the defendant chased up from behind and slapped me twice. The fourth time I went to deliver the judgment, I accompanied the 14th bailiff. The defendant threw the judgment on the ground and spoke insults. When I wanted to call the police station, the defendant took the opportunity to escape. Many female relatives made things difficult for us, and a man wearing a coat said that killing a person in the court was like killing a dog, and it would cost at most 300 yuan to settle it." Then, the defendant Chen Huazhang testified that he had been smoking opium due to illness, and denied insulting court personnel. But "Mr. Wang scolded me for being a fool. One night, it was already past 9:00, and he broke into my house. I don't know what he meant." After verifying the testimony, the court ruled that the case still needed to be investigated, so it was ordered to postpone the interrogation. The defendant was ordered to pay a cash bail of 1,000 yuan to be released pending further instructions. If no bail was provided, he would be detained. The defendant, upon hearing the order, immediately took out a large wad of banknotes, counted 1,000 yuan to pay for the bail, and left the court.

Husband Commits a Crime and is Imprisoned, Wife Files for Divorce 157

Xia Desheng, a local resident, is only nineteen years old. He does not think about studying and is willing to engage in depravity. He associates with a group of bandits. Recently, his father, Xia Yongxiang, published an announcement expelling him, declaring that he was severing the relationship between father and son. Last month, Xia Desheng and Liu Yunting were reported for extortion and were arrested by the local court. After questioning, it was confirmed that the two criminals, Xia Desheng and Liu Yunting, were each sentenced to two months of imprisonment. Now, Xia Desheng's wife, Ma Suzhu, hired lawyer Pan Zhensheng and filed for divorce in the mediation court of the local court. The reasons are abuse, abandonment, and neglect of alimony, and she also requests payment of 360 yuan in alimony. Yesterday, Judge Yao Fuxiang summoned Ma Suzhu and her lawyer Pan to court. Ma Suzhu testified that she was sixteen years old when she married Xia Desheng on January 10th, 22nd year of the Republic, through a matchmaker and under her mother's order. At first, she lived with her in-laws, but Xia Desheng was a romantic villain with no legitimate occupation. He wasted money outside and often pawned my clothes for expenses. If he was not satisfied, he would beat and abuse me. Afterwards, he apologized and wrote a handwritten note as proof. Later, Xia Desheng was expelled from the family for not listening to his parents. In the summer of this year, Xia Desheng took me to rent a house on Miller Road in Hongkou to live together, but he had no source of income for rent and other expenses. All my clothes were pawned. On the 13th day of the ninth lunar month, Xia Desheng said goodbye to the petitioner and left, saying, "I am really sorry for you. I am going to Nanjing to join the army. It is difficult to determine when I will return." He left a photo and twenty-three pawn tickets before leaving. At this point, I could only cry and wash my face with tears. I was alone and had no idea what to do. I had no choice but to pawn my dowry items, such as dressing tables and washstands, to take care of all the debts and live temporarily in my mother's house alone. I deeply regret meeting the wrong person and resent my whole life. I am also pregnant and cannot work to earn a living, which makes me feel even more difficult. Now I know that Xia Desheng was recently arrested for extortion with others and sentenced to imprisonment. Therefore, my hope for my husband is completely cut off." The judge ordered the detained Xia Desheng to be brought to court to testify. He said, "If she wants a divorce, I can't stop her. I can only let her be free. As for asking me to pay alimony, I am unable to afford it." The judge asked Ma Suzhu, who also voluntarily gave up the alimony. The judge considered that the conciliation was successful and drafted a conciliation record in court, ordering both parties to sign it and leave the court.

They let the bandits search and plunder. After about half an hour, they left satisfied. Checking the losses, it was about 200 yuan. He immediately reported to the police station in charge and requested a pursuit, but a happy occasion was thus disintegrated, and everyone returned with their heads lowered and crestfallen.

Shanghai-Minlong Distance Buses Collect Tolls 160

The Shanghai-Minlong-Nanzhe long-distance bus company in this city is now following the third article, second item of the Five Provinces and Cities Transportation Committee's revised Commercial Automobile Road Company's toll collection rules for commercial vehicles, as well as the Public Works Bureau's restrictions on the number of passengers on large commercial vehicles, transit methods, and toll collection as follows: 2 yuan for 8 to 14 people, 3 yuan for 15 to 21 people, 4 yuan for 22 to 28 people, and 5 yuan for 29 to 35 people. Calculated on a round-trip basis, any violation of the above methods, exceeding the limit, or transporting goods in passenger vehicles is not allowed to pass, etc.

Seeking Clues from an Adulterous Woman

Huang Ruiting, from Ningbo, served as a translator in the Vehicle Department of the Public Concession Public Works Bureau. Last year, Huang took advantage of his position to make agreements with rickshaw merchants Gu Songmao and others to solicit bribes as the price for not being demanding when inspecting vehicles. At that time, Gu had paid 1,200 foreign dollars three times. Later, the head of the Vehicle Department, a Westerner, found out about it. Huang, seeing that the incident was exposed, also abandoned his post and fled. Recently, the chief inspector of the General Patrol House, Lu Liankui, detective Wu Hanzhang, and others arrested him and filed a public prosecution with the First Special Court for the crime of fraud under Article 336 of the Criminal Law. After the interrogation was concluded, he was awaiting sentencing. Yesterday morning, British Judge of the First Special Court opened the Fifth Criminal Court and announced the judgment. Huang Ruiting was sentenced to four months of imprisonment for fraud and fined 300 yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be one day of imprisonment for two days.

Pregnant Woman and Midwife Take Coal Briquettes for Warming, Almost Losing Their Lives 163

Zhang Lianzhi, a resident of No. 18 Local House, Luoxiang, Hudong District, is from Yangzhou and works as a worker in the Yangshupu Yarn Factory. He married Shen, who is now 25 years old and pregnant at full term. She suddenly gave birth a few days ago and hired midwife He to deliver the baby. Because the weather was cold, she burned a charcoal stove for warming. Unexpectedly, the house was short and narrow, with no doors or windows, and the stove was very hot, causing poisoning. At that time, Chen's sister happened to enter the room to shop and saw her sister-in-law lying stiffly on the bed, the midwife fainted and fell to the ground, and the baby was also suffocated and silent. She felt the coal gas choking her and was unbearably suffocated, so she shouted for help. Neighbors gathered. At that time, Lianzhi happened to return home from work and saw the situation. For a moment, he did not know what to do. Fortunately, a neighbor immediately went to the Hongkou Public Obstetrics Clinic at the intersection of Huade Road and hired doctors Wang Ying and Xu Cuizhen to rush to the rescue. Fortunately, the poisoning was still mild, and the pregnant woman and the midwife woke up one after another. The baby was half purple, and although artificial respiration was used to treat it, it was already in a terrible state.

Arts and Entertainment 167

The Bright Harmonica Team Holds its Second Concert

A preview of the Bright Harmonica Team, Shanghai’s only distinguished amateur group. Henan Province Extends Winter Vacation 169

Hebei Schools Hold Final Exams 170

(Tianjin, 13th Dispatch) High schools and above in Hebei province will hold final exams starting from the 14th. Winter vacation will begin on the 18th and last for two weeks.

Ministry of Education Explains High School Freshman Admission Qualifications 171

The Ministry of Education, in response to a request from the Shaanxi Education Department for clarification regarding high school freshman admission qualifications, specifically instructed the department, stating that students who have studied in junior high school for three years but have not participated in the school's graduation examination or the joint examination, or who have failed three subjects in the joint examination and should repeat a grade, as well as graduates or students from unregistered private secondary schools, if they are admitted to the Shaanxi Provincial Xi’an Senior High School with equivalent academic qualifications, should be approved for filing. However, the proportion of enrolled students should be subject to the restrictions of Article 72, Paragraph 2 of the Secondary School Regulations (the proportion of new students with equivalent academic qualifications admitted to secondary schools should not exceed 20% of the total enrollment for high schools and 30% for junior high schools. It should be determined by the education administrative departments of each province and city, considering local conditions, and reported to the Ministry of Education for record).

Ministry of Education Explains the Qualifications for Primary School Principals Serving as Acting Principals 172

The Ministry of Education telegraphed the Hebei Provincial Education Department, stating that if primary school principals appointed before the promulgation of the primary school regulations do not meet the qualifications stipulated in the regulations, they may be allowed to continue serving until the end of the academic year. After completing their term of office, if they have achieved good results during their tenure and possess one of the qualifications listed in Article 78 of the primary school regulations ((1) Graduation: from schools above the old-style middle school or senior high school, having served as a primary school teacher for more than one year, or having completed educational coursework at summer schools run by local educational administrative departments or university education colleges, normal schools, etc., for two summer periods; (2) Graduation: from two-year or more normal training courses or simple normal schools’ simple normal courses, having served as a primary school teacher for more than two years, or having completed supplementary studies at the aforementioned summer schools for three summer periods; (3) Having served as a primary school teacher for more than three years and having been recognized by the educational administrative department as having achieved good results, or having completed supplementary studies at the aforementioned summer schools for four summer periods; (4) Having served as a primary school teacher for more than three years and having published specialized works on primary school education, which have been recognized by the competent educational administrative department as having real value), they may be deemed qualified without examination. If there are no suitable personnel to replace them for the time being, they may be appointed as acting principals in accordance with the provisions of Article 83 of the primary school regulations regarding substitute teachers (if a primary school cannot hire teachers with the qualifications stipulated in Article 75 or who have passed the examination due to special local circumstances, those who possess one of the qualifications stipulated in Article 79 may be used as substitute teachers, but it should be submitted to the competent educational administrative department for approval). They may be approved by the department to serve as acting principals and temporarily allowed to continue serving until a new principal is appointed. If there is no candidate who meets the qualifications stipulated in Article 81 of the primary school regulations (teachers who possess one of the qualifications in Article 75 or who have passed the examination and have served for more than two years and have achieved good results may serve as primary school principals; Article 75 refers to graduates of the education departments of normal universities and university education colleges, graduates of higher normal schools or specialized normal schools, and graduates of old-style normal school undergraduate courses or senior high school normal courses or special normal courses, who may serve as grade teachers or specialized teachers), those who possess one of the qualifications stipulated in Article 79 may be temporarily appointed on a trial basis, also known as acting principals. If the above two types of acting principals serve for two years and achieve good results, they may be converted into formal principals.

Qinghai Education Department Requests Commendation for Ma Bufang's Establishment of Education for All Ethnic Groups 173

The Ministry of Education recently received a report from Yang Xirao, the Director of the Qinghai Provincial Education Department, stating that Qinghai is located in a remote border area with backward culture and that educational facilities face many difficulties. Since the establishment of the province, Chairman Ma has relied on his great strategy and planning to vigorously promote education for all ethnic groups, including Mongol, Tibetan, Hui, and Han, in order to consolidate the foundation of border defense. However, due to recent droughts and floods, uneven distribution of water and frequent hailstorms, people's livelihoods are exhausted, causing farmers and merchants to suffer, and the province's finances are stagnant. The current situation is difficult to maintain, and all matters that should be developed have not been carried out in order. In recent years, the central government has paid attention to the Northwest and implemented development. Party and government officials have visited Qinghai many times to investigate, and they all believe that cultural backwardness is a major shortcoming of Qinghai Province. Therefore, Ma Bufang, the commander of the Second Army of the Central Army and the commander of the Hainan Garrison, resolutely used military industrial policies in the autumn of 1934 to build the Qinghai Library and the affiliated middle school of the Islamic Promotion Association on a large scale. He also established well-equipped Mongol, Tibetan, and Hui primary schools affiliated with the garrison command and established Mongol and Tibetan primary schools in Dulan County, far from the provincial capital. Such selflessness and impartiality, regardless of boundaries, and the establishment of a grand library to promote culture in the face of extreme economic difficulties are rare among military and police leaders in the border provinces and even rare among military commanders across the country. If a special commendation is not requested, it will not be enough to highlight public virtue and encourage future generations. In response to the report, the Ministry of Education, in addition to sending a letter of encouragement from Minister of Education Wang Shijie, also instructed that future border education should focus on developing resources, cultivating production, and uniting all ethnic groups to consolidate border defense.

Ministry of Education Hires Yan Jialin to Plan National Children's Training 174

Since the promulgation of the junior high school curriculum standards, the Ministry of Education has decided to replace military training with Boy Scout training, which shows the importance it attaches to children's training. Therefore, a Boy Scout instructor training class was held during the summer vacation last year, and fifteen directors of the National Boy Scout Council were hired to establish the National Boy Scout General Association. Since the Ministry has made children's training a compulsory course for junior high schools, specialized personnel are needed to manage the Boy Scout curriculum and various regulations. Recently, due to President Dai's recommendation, Yan Jialin was hired as a special editor. Mr. Yan arrived at the Ministry at the end of December last year to negotiate and settle matters. It is decided that after completing his original position at Huazhong University in Wuhan this month, he will go to the Ministry to take office.

Jiangsu Social Education Facilities () 186

(Report by Zhou Fo-hai, Director of the Jiangsu Education Department, at the Provincial Government's Memorial Week)

Jiangsu's social education has made considerable progress in the past two years. According to recent statistics, the total expenditure on social education in various counties of Jiangsu Province amounts to 1,396,124 yuan. The provincial education funds allocated to social education are also 567,462 yuan, totaling 1,963,586 yuan. The social education institutions run by various counties include 151 public education centers, 141 farmer education centers, 41 libraries, 70 sports grounds, 17 public education experimental zones, 475 public reading rooms, and 121 other social education institutions, totaling 1,015 institutions. Various counties have 1,651 public schools, comprising 1,225 classes, with a total of 70,128 students. Compared to the 19th and 20th years of the Republic, there has been a significant increase. Back then, the total social education expenditure in various counties of the province was only over 1.31 million, and the counties only had more than 130 public education centers and more than 80 farmer education centers. Other institutions were also not as numerous as they are now. However, given that Jiangsu has spent so much money and established so many institutions, what is the state of these facilities, what are the effects, and how should they be improved in the future? A thorough examination should be conducted. A report is now presented separately as follows:

When I first came to Jiangsu, many people expressed dissatisfaction with Jiangsu's social education, saying that social education institutions were just taking money and not doing anything, as if they were retirement homes. When I looked at the inspection reports of social education in various counties, I realized that many of these criticisms were indeed factual. After much observation, I realized that there were four main reasons why Jiangsu's social education was so debilitated. First, the scope of work of social education institutions was too broad and lacked specific standards, so that they tried to do everything at the beginning, and as a result, nothing was done successfully. Second, in the past, the allocation of funds for social education institutions lacked specific standards, so most of the funds were used for salaries, and there was no way to carry out any projects. Third, in the past, the staff of social education institutions mostly lacked a thorough understanding of their responsibilities, so their work inevitably contained errors. Fourth, in the past, educational administrative agencies only focused on expanding social education as much as possible, and failed to pay enough attention to quality improvement, resulting in procrastination and complacency becoming a habit. Because I knew the reasons for the debilitation of social education in Jiangsu, the authorities immediately decided to focus on strengthening, rectifying, and evaluating work through administrative power. At that time, three key points were also decided. First, the standard for the allocation of funds for social education institutions was determined, that is, salaries should not be higher than 50%, project funds should not be lower than 40%, and administrative expenses should be 10%, to ensure that the projects carried out by various institutions can be carried out one after another. Second, important regulations such as the detailed rules of service and the evaluation procedures for directors and staff of social education institutions in various counties were formulated, and it was strictly ordered that directors and staff of social education institutions should not hold concurrent positions, so that all social education institutions would be responsible for planning and implementing the popularization and promotion of social education in their respective areas. Other social education institutions within the area must also be responsible for guidance, and the central institutions must also contact each other to jointly seek the improvement of social education in the entire county. After this method was stipulated, most counties were able to earnestly comply with it, and various social education institutions were also able to consciously strive for improvement. Now, many counties have established a social education center in each autonomous region, and some counties have not been able to do so due to economic reasons, but they will continue to promote this year by year in order to complete it.

New World Record in 100-Meter Breaststroke 194

(Havas News Agency, Providence, USA) A new world record in the 100-meter breaststroke was set at a local university sports meet. The new record holder is a university student named John Hachens, who broke the world record of 1 minute 13.6 seconds set by France's Catonnat in 1932 with a time of 1 minute 11.8 seconds.

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Heaven

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seven: Hearing Words, Hiding Tears to Sell Oneself and Lament Bitterness; Carefully Peering at Invitation Cards, Eagerly Seeking Refuge

Li Shilian waited for him to write the words on the acknowledgement slip, handed it over, and then smiled: Speaking of affection, Mr. Cheng is really something. Although he gave them two dollars, he didn't expect any benefits, just giving two dollars to help them survive. This is called bestowing kindness without expecting repayment. Apart from older people who are truly cultivating themselves, who can do that? Mr. Cheng is really worthy of admiration. As he said this, he stretched out both hands and held up two thumbs. Cheng Zhiqian smiled: If you say I'm affectionate, I won't admit it. If you say I'm a busybody, I'll admit it. As he spoke, he looked at Wang Beihai, wanting to ask him to bring the draft calculations he had brought. Li Shilian, however, did not want to leave immediately. He wanted to find out how his relationship with Director Gao was. He adopted a respectful attitude, bending his body slightly even while sitting, and asked with a smile: Mr. Cheng, your arrival in Xi'an has brought a lot of glory to those of us from the East, and you are welcomed everywhere. As for us, it's impossible to ask someone for even a bite to eat. Isn't it extremely shameful? Cheng Zhiqian smiled and said: It's nothing really. Because there are two officials here who are old friends of mine, and through their introductions, I've gotten to know more people. For officials, entertaining guests is unavoidable. It doesn't hurt to bring me along to dinner. For example, tonight, Gao Hesheng is hosting a dinner for Yuan Youwei's younger brother. He can't just invite his two brothers to eat a whole table of food, so he has to find more people to fill the table. So, bringing us along not only doesn't take anything away from him but also implies that we're helping him out. But then again, the fact that he's willing to have us help him out means he thinks highly of me. Otherwise, as a director in Xi'an City, he's a second-class wealthy person, and people would be rushing to show their respect. (112)

Zhabei 195

— Ding Weinan

Here, the scarlet blood of our compatriots was once smeared; it endured the artillery fire and bombs of the tyrannical sun; it was imprinted with the traces of wooden sandals. The scene is filled with rubble and withered grass, and the setting sun shines on it, causing the flowing wind to stir up dust. The desolate appearance makes people unable to help but shed tears! There are no complete houses, only scattered and broken remains, crippled walls, and charred buildings – all surrounded by utter devastation! Quiet and miserable, it seems that this is not a world for people.

How long has it been? And this place is no longer what it was then! We can see new buildings, very smooth roads, and bustling pedestrians; the wailing of cars brings back the atmosphere of the city that had once died. Inside the fence made of bamboo, the songs of rebirth sound out. The painful scars are healing.

At night, we can also see moving neon lights, although this is not like the "Concession," which has sleepless streets, Europeans, Americans, foreign bastards, and Japanese brothels. There are also enchanting eyes and smiling faces, as well as white eyes and depressed faces. But here, in this "Zhabei" that was once sacrificed, this northern part of Shanghai city, the "Chinese territory" that the Chinese often talk about, naturally still has some urban qualities, although it can't catch up with the "foreign territory" that the Chinese often talk about, which is so prosperous and lively. But it's still not bad. Although this newly healed patient is still lacking in health, the doctor's surgery will not have been in vain!

However, scars cover the whole body. The scars of one or two wounds can be treated, but how can the shadow of humiliation above them be erased? This must be asked of those compatriots who have not died!

(Snippets) 196

— (Xiong Yu)

Glass breaks instantly when hit by a stone; wood is easily split when met with iron. Examining their physical properties, one lacks cohesive force and is not united, and is trampled upon; the other is rich in cohesive force and is solid and united, making it impossible for people to start. Therefore, people also value unity. In large cases, it is the whole country; in small cases, it is a family, only then will they be spared from being insulted.

Foreign Beggars 197

— Yun Xun

Hongkou is the Japanese expatriate district of Shanghai. From time to time, you see monks from that country who don't knock on wooden fish but beat small drums, banging and clanging non-stop. Based on figurative speculation, it is naturally like Chinese monks begging for alms; some people call them foreign monks. Foreign monks also hold onto the devoutness of their beliefs. They travel back and forth on the concrete roads, which are two hundred yards long. The difference between them and Chinese monks is only in the speed of their steps. They stride like the wind, while we move slowly like yellow oxen plowing the fields. Monks have no ethnic boundaries, but in spirit, there is a clear distinction.

Recently, I saw a true foreign beggar on Christmas! Jesus's Christmas! Before that day, Christians were already preparing for a passionate, unrestrained celebration. Messengers in green were working harder for Christmas, delivering blessings in greeting cards. Department stores were decorating with many stories of Santa Claus for Christmas, advertising their products. At this time, western bums took advantage of the opportunity to dress up as Santa Claus in the Nanjing and Huilu company area, seemingly with the sincere intention of Jesus saving the world, blessing various shops. The white, long beard fluttered across the chest, with silver hair all over the head, wearing a red scarf, and a brand-new scarlet robe with white edges. I glanced over from the tram car, as if he was holding a piece of chalk in his hand, writing words of blessing on the glass window of the shop! Curious people followed a large crowd to watch the excitement, and there were also two Indian police officers maintaining order. After the blessing words were written, naturally there would be a "reaching out General!" This is exactly the same as on the night of the twenty-fourth day of the twelfth lunar month in the mainland, when beggars dressed up as the Kitchen God in advance and "jump the Kitchen God" along the street; shouting loudly: "The Kitchen God is here, the boss's business is buzzing!" (meaning prosperous). Jump left and get rich! Jump right and get rich! Not jumping also gets rich! Followed by three cannons, ...tong, ...tong, ...tong; after the auspicious words were finished, it was also "reaching out General;" however, it is a bit blasphemous to the Holy Lord and the gods to use the fake Jesus Kitchen God as a front for begging.

Records of Fleeting Fragrance from the Imperial Incense 198

— Original by Princess Der Ling of Qing, Translated by Qin Shouou

The distance between them was about a foot and a half, but it could be wider or narrower, as they were not tied down by anything, just hanging in the air. I stared at them for a good while, unable to figure out whether they were decorations or tools; and if they were tools, what were they used for? Finally, I couldn't hold back any longer and respectfully asked the Empress Dowager.

She first smiled at me proudly, and this smile clearly indicated that she had a true understanding of this strange object, thanks to reading more books or listening to people talk about it; so I stood up attentively, ready to receive her grand instruction.

"This thing certainly has its use!" Her first sentence made it clear to me that it was a tool, not a decoration. "But to explain its use," she added, "we must first go to the back to take a look!"

With that, she waved to the person in charge of the archery range—who was also an official. This person hurried forward, approached the back door, removed the bolt, and pushed both doors open at once. He then stepped aside. A rectangular open space appeared before our eyes, its end about thirty or forty zhang away from where we were standing. Opposite us was a tall, massive stone wall, with a few trees and small houses planted on both sides, presumably the residences of the people in charge of the archery range. In the center was a stone-free path five or six zhang wide; it must have been very flat before, but now it was covered with weeds. (222)

Talking About Advertising 199

— Yun

Advertising is a necessary weapon in the commercial battle, and also the second life of a store. Whether a store is large or small, if it is not good at advertising, then even if the goods are piled up like mountains, no one will inquire about them, and the result will inevitably be closure due to unbearable losses. Therefore, general stores all attach extreme importance to advertising. However, in the writing of advertisements, some exaggerate too much, causing readers to lose faith, while others are too honest, lacking gimmicks, and thus lose the effectiveness of advertising. Therefore, writing advertisements must indeed consider all aspects. For example, Tian Xiaode Fur Bureau published a huge advertisement, wildly exaggerating about a disastrous drop in prices, falling into the core of its capital. If that were really the case, I'm afraid other fur stores would have to close. I wanted to buy a fur coat, and because I saw the advertisement for Tian Xiaode Fur Bureau, stating that a blue fox coat priced over a thousand yuan was now selling for less than two-tenths of the original price, I couldn't help but be moved. I went to buy one in person, but after seeing the goods, I was greatly disappointed! It turned out that this fur bureau, which hadn't really fallen into the core of its capital, was only charging high prices. Therefore, I dared not take advantage of this "bargain" and, as a result, thought about the advertisement. If it's described too extravagantly, not only will it fail to attract customers, but it may also lose their faith, and everyone will scold them as a slippery Tian Xiaode!

Miscellaneous Talk

American Husband, Japanese Wife 200

— Shazhou

In the world, American husbands are the best, and Japanese wives are the best—this is a well-known fact.

Kushida Hakuson tells us in "Impressions of North America":

"Two people walk in shoulder to shoulder, intimately and with smiles, and sit in a fixed position in the dining hall. This is the French style. The husband walks in front, hands in his pockets, glancing left and right, chest proudly puffed out, and the wife follows behind. This is the English style. Now, look! In America, the wife enters majestically, bestowing a glance upon her subjects to the left and right, and takes her throne first. The husband follows later—this is the American style." Is this the only good thing about American husbands? The answer is "no." Then please say a little more.

To talk about the good things about American husbands, they are truly extraordinarily good. If you don't believe it, look at the evenings on holidays. Who is at home playing with the children, patiently waiting for his "dear" until the night is late? Is it the man or the woman? According to our Chinese custom, it is of course the woman. But if you say it's the woman, you're wrong. It turns out that the woman goes out to socialize, and the man stays at home to wait. That is the American custom, and it can be said to be an iron rule that cannot be changed. But is it just waiting at the door? Not at all. No matter how tired he is, almost falling asleep, as soon as he hears the doorbell ring, he will immediately go to the door cheerfully to open it. The elegant wife walks in, and he lets her go first, then closes the door and follows behind. When they reach the room, the woman lifts her foot, and the man skillfully says, "Yes, dear." As he says this, he immediately takes off the woman's arched shoes. At that time, he has to be careful not to let his nose get hit by the shoes, because the woman lifts her foot too close to the man's nose.

When going out on the street, the man follows behind the woman, carrying her coat and the items she bought. If there are children, he also has to push the stroller. If the woman's shoelaces come undone, the man also has to run two steps ahead to tie them up.

At home, when his wife is talking to her friends, the man has no right to speak. If he wants to speak, he must first ask the Queen for permission. All of these things are too numerous to mention. Fortunately, I am not writing a "Guide to American Husbands" here, so omitting some things is not likely to be harmful.

So what about Japanese wives? Quite coincidentally, they are in stark contrast to American wives. Brewing tea, cooking rice, taking care of children, washing clothes, sweeping the floor... there is nothing that is not a woman's job. If a man has guests, it is the woman's job to kneel and offer fragrant tea to the guests. It is also something a woman cannot object to if her husband pawns her pants to get money for him to go to prostitutes.

I once read an article recently published on "Truetoty" titled "I Married a Japanese Man." It was a story about an American woman who married a Japanese man and suffered endless contempt and hardship. As an American woman living the bitter life of a Japanese wife, we can naturally imagine what it's like.

What about Chinese couples? Is the husband a slave to the wife, or is the wife a slave to the husband? We only need to observe the facts a little to answer very straightforwardly: those at the forefront of the trend are American, and those who are behind the times are still thoroughly Chinese. (Japan is the descendant of Xu Fu of our country, so China and Japan are similar.) Which is right and which is wrong is something for specialized scholars to study. I have only fulfilled a bit of the responsibility of introducing it. However, before getting married, please first decide in your heart what kind of husband or wife you want to be.

Rumors of Financial Loans Re-emerge, Target Price Tries to Rise but Lacks Power 201

—Resulting in a Reversal and a Drop of One Yuan One One—

Yesterday, the gold market's upward trend was once again hindered due to the re-emergence of rumors of loans and the hardening of the foreign exchange market, resulting in a mid-course reversal. The Central Bank took advantage of the low prices to open spot trading, and gradually stabilized after the low. In the morning, overseas silver markets were flat in British currency but shrunk in American currency. The forward silver price at Mont-de-Pieté rose slightly. There were both rises and falls in foreign exchange rates. The price of London raw gold fell two pence. The off-exchange preliminary transaction opened and immediately rose to 63.34 yuan. Buyers surged in, and it rose again to 63.45 yuan. The Central Bank's listed price was announced, with British currency flat and American currency up 1.875. The Customs Gold Unit fell three thousandths, and the target price standard price retreated to 997 yuan, without much impact. The situation remained stable. After opening, due to rumors that a certain bank was borrowing 500,000 pounds from a certain Western merchant, selling pressure suddenly increased and gradually retreated to within 60 yuan. Buyers were active in taking advantage of the low prices, maintaining the market to some extent. However, the foreign exchange market hardened due to West Merchant Sassoon's tendency to fulfill spot orders first, and large players re-emerged, causing a one-time drop. But because the Central Bank opened spot trading at a target price of 957 yuan, confidence was boosted, and buyers continued to be active, gradually rising back to above 61 yuan. The announcement of the silver equalization tax remained unchanged. At this point, supply and demand were balanced, and the market was sluggish. Although it broke the 60 yuan mark again due to floating profits being closed out after entering, the buying interest of large players gradually increased, and the foreign exchange market had turned stable. Although there were fluctuations in the middle, the overall trend was mediocre, without much change. At noon, the phenomenon of banks having a buying appetite turned the situation prosperous, and large players came back to buy. In the afternoon, the market tended to be firm. Banks took advantage of the situation to fulfill orders, and the foreign exchange market still had a tendency to loosen. With supply exceeding demand in the market, large players entered and then exited. The gold market then turned from high to fall, but confidence was still stable. Buyers were active in taking advantage of the low prices, making it easy to pull up the market. Although Indian silver initially reported a rise of nine annas, there was a slight decline. However, because the Central Bank continued to open spot trading, the price was maintained at 959 yuan. Thereafter, there was limited trading in the market. Although there was a rebound, it soon declined slightly again. Finally, Indian silver declined slightly by two annas, and the gold market entered a dull state. Starting at 3:00 p.m. today, February term rollover trading will be held, with the premium estimated to be advanced by the short side by about 6-7 yuan, depending entirely on the strength of the long side. Now, the day's market conditions are recorded as follows: the morning opening was 964.4 yuan, an increase of 0.7 yuan compared to last week. It was not like the previous crazy high, which shocked people, and no one paid attention to the current big drop. When the foreign interest rate was crazily high, the silver root was tight and the sellers were enthusiastic. When the foreign interest rate fell sharply, the silver root was not seen to be loose. Therefore, the bulls were content, and the large number of shorts released last time had no intention of hedging. The retail arbitrage transactions last time were also not seen to be swapped. In terms of chip supply and demand, the supply was still greater than the demand. Therefore, it was temporarily unable to invigorate. The future of the market price, hoping for a big rise, depends on whether the retail hedging is consistently swapped and whether the large shorts rise up to hedge. Otherwise, relying solely on sporadic entry and exit, even if it does not decline, it will not be able to get out of the hovering state. Oil Market: Sichuan Exchange Rate Soars, Tung Oil 218

Foreign firms in Hankou have a long history of establishing plantations in Chongqing and Wanxian in Sichuan Province to purchase white tung oil. During this peak season for new goods, foreign firms are competing to purchase. White tung oil is one of the largest products of Sichuan Province, truly worthy of being a region blessed by nature. However, financial relations with other provinces have historically been isolated. Recently, the Sichuan exchange rate has suddenly soared, now reaching 1,680 yuan. The internal financial panic is imaginable. As a result, it is difficult for foreign firms to purchase tung oil from the producing areas. Some are observing, and some are abandoning purchases. The majority are turning to Hankou and Changde in Hunan Province to purchase. Hankou and Changde are now seeing a shortage of supply. Therefore, merchants in Hankou have been importing goods from other places in recent days, and prices are increasing daily. Previously, foreign firms in Hankou were selling at 31 yuan per dan. That price is now a thing of the past. Considering the current imports, the price at foreign firms must be 32 yuan. Although there have been no transactions, a storm is brewing. Considering this, the market will continue to rise, and the situation is evident. Since the Hankou market is like this, Zhejiang tung oil is also affected and following suit. The asking price in Hangzhou was 26 yuan per stone the day before yesterday, and the market now has to increase the price. In general, foreign firms have a strong demand for goods, and demand everywhere exceeds supply. What is most difficult is that this year is a drought year. The oil produced in drought-stricken areas is not up to the standards required by foreign firms. Therefore, it is even more difficult to find goods suitable for export. The quality standards of foreign firms are extremely strict, requiring 1.5170, or at least 1.5168. However, most of the oil produced in drought-stricken areas this year is between 1.5154 and 1.5. Therefore, goods that meet the standards are even more scarce and valuable.

Silk and Tea: Little Silk in Stock, Easy to Trade, and Clear 219

There is not much silk in stock in Shanghai, and market prices have risen accordingly. Trading was once booming. Although telegrams from overseas indicate prices 30-40 yuan lower, the local market in this city remains robust. Recently, the number of goods advanced by stockpilers has been large. The number of goods required for textile production by silk stocking factories and those purchased in advance (silk stocking factories typically purchase goods in advance at the beginning of the year or because there is no formal market at the beginning of the new year) is also similar. Silk merchants are also holding firm on prices, resulting in no transactions in recent days. Both buyers and sellers seem to be temporarily taking a wait-and-see approach.
